For example, title-case operation will change to upper-case all the characters immediately after the period (.), dash (-), underscore (_), and whitespace characters. Then it comes back working with that unique temporary name, and determine whether to leave as that name currently is, or change to your desired name.\r\n\r\nThis explanation might seem lengthy and complicated, but the case is not common, but also can happen so it needs to be mentioned. The abort operation can result in that unique naming, so don’t abort if you don’t really need to.
